***pip.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pip.html>pip</a> (12521)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pip.html>pip</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:disease.html>disease</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:poultry.html>poultry</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:also.html>also</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:people.html>people</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> post-classical <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pipita</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pītuīta</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:slime.html>slime</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:head.html>head</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:cold.html>cold</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_9"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pip.html>pip</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:pip.html>Pip</a></a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:any.html>any</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:various.html>various</a> respiratory diseases <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:especially.html>especially</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:infectious.html>infectious</a> coryza).</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:humorous.html>humorous</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>Of</a> humans, <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:disease.html>disease</a> (particularly <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:common.html>common</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:cold.html>cold</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:flu.html>flu</a>), <a href = vnd.unilang:malaise.html>malaise</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:depression.html>depression</a>.</li></ol>
